    function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match('(?:^|;)\\s*' + name + '=([^;]*)');

        return (match) ? decodeURIComponent(match[1]) : null;
    }

    function extractUserId() {
        return getCookie("userId");
    }

        if (raw) {

        }

        return (match) ? match[1] : "";
    }

    function googlead()
    {

    function sendUserTiming(category, variable, value, label) {
        var args = arguments;
        if (args.length < 3 || args.length > 4) {
            throw new Error('Invalid arguments amount!');
        }

        ga('send', 'timing', category, variable, Math.round(value), label);
    }

            ga('set', 'dimension15', userId);

            var clientId = Services.ClientIdService.extractClientId();

       var AP = AP || {};
AP.cmd = AP.cmd || [];

AP.cmd.push(function(container) {
    var rootDomain = "/";

    function startCustomSearch() {
        if (!CustomSearch) {
            return setTimeout(startCustomSearch, 13);
        }

        new CustomSearch($('#ac_search'), {
            'rootDomain': rootDomain,
            'searchUrl': rootDomain + 'api/v2/search/',
            'logUrl': rootDomain + 'search/query_save/',
            'searchTitle': 'Search',
            'containerSearch': '.custom-search-js',
            'searchButton': '#customSearchButton',
            'container': container
        });
    }

    startCustomSearch();
});

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var AP = AP || {};
AP.cmd = AP.cmd || [];

AP.cmd.push(function(container) {
    var widgetStorageKey = 'widget_buy_closed';

    var storage = new AP.SessionStorage();
    var widgetBuyClosed = storage.get(widgetStorageKey);

    if (!widgetBuyClosed) {

        var $widgetBlock = $('[data-widget="widget_buy"]');
        var $widgetTemplate = $('#widget_top-buy');

        $widgetTemplate.tmpl().appendTo($widgetBlock);
        $widgetBlock.slideDown('500');

        var $widgetClose = $('[data-widget-close]', $widgetBlock);
        var $widgetBody = $('[data-widget-body]', $widgetBlock);

        var $displayButton = $('[data-widget-head]', $widgetBlock).on('click', function() {
            $(this).slideUp();
            $widgetBody.slideDown();
            $widgetClose.show();
            container.get('hint_service').updatePositions();
        });

        $('[data-widget-close]', $widgetBlock).on('click', function() {
            $widgetBlock.slideUp('200');
            storage.set(widgetStorageKey, true);
        });

    }
});
     </script>

         <script type="text/javascript">
          var AP = AP || {};
AP.cmd = AP.cmd || [];

AP.cmd.push(function(container) {
    container.get("render_select").onReady(function() {
        initBrandFilter();
    });


    function initBrandFilter() {
        var $findByBrand = $("#brand_filter");
        var $brands =  $findByBrand.find('[name="brand"]');
        var $models =  $findByBrand.find("select[name='model']");
        var $allModels = $models.find("option[data-brand]");
        var $optGroup = $models.find("optgroup");
        var catalogPath =  $findByBrand.find('[name="catalog"]').val();

        var router = container.get("router");

        $findByBrand.on("submit", function(event) {
            event.preventDefault();

            var result = router.generate("finderIndexPage", {
                "catalogPath": "newcars"
            });
            var brandPath = $brands.val();
            var modelPath = $models.val();
            if (brandPath && !modelPath) {
                result = router.generate("brandPage", {
                    "catalogPath": catalogPath,
                    "brandPath": brandPath
                });
            }

            if (brandPath && modelPath) {
                result = router.generate("modelPage", {
                    "catalogPath": catalogPath,
                    "brandPath": brandPath,
                    "modelPath": modelPath
                });
            }

            window.location.href = result;
        });

        $brands.on("change", function() {
            $models.val("");
            $optGroup.detach();

            if (this.value == "") {
                $models.attr("disabled", "disabled");
                $allModels.detach();
            } else {
                var _brand = '[data-brand="' + this.value + '"]';
                var _not_brand = ':not([data-brand="' + this.value + '"])';
                $models.removeAttr("disabled", "disabled");
                $allModels.filter(_not_brand).detach();
                $allModels.filter(_brand).not("[data-upcoming]").appendTo($models);
                $allModels.filter(_brand).filter("[data-upcoming]").appendTo($optGroup);
                if ($optGroup.children().length > 0) {
                    $optGroup.appendTo($models);
                }
            }
        }).removeAttr('disabled');
    }
});

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var AP = AP || {};
AP.cmd = AP.cmd || [];

AP.cmd.push(function(app) {
    var $owl;

    $owl = $('.js-carousel-trending-cars');

    $owl.on('initialized.owl.carousel', function(e) {
        var owlInstance = e.relatedTarget;
        var previousPosition = 1;

        $(this).on('click', '.owl-next', function() {
            if (owlInstance._current == previousPosition) {
                owlInstance.to(0, 250, true);
            }

            previousPosition = owlInstance._current;
        });
    });

    $owl.owlCarousel({
        stagePadding: 50,
        margin: 0,
        dots: false,
        autoWidth: true,
        item: 10,
        nav: true
    });
});
     </script>

       <h2 class="h2 m_b-15 capitalize">

       </h2>
       <div class="recently-viewed cell-sm" data-loader="asyncLoader" data-slot="recently-viewed" data-type="lazyRender">
       </div>
       <script data-template="recently-viewed-cars" type="text/x-tmpl">
        {{if (models.length > 0)}}
            <div class="carousel_model-row"><div class="carousel_model carousel_recently_cars owl-carousel" id="movieListBag" data-gtm-collection="impressions">

                    {{tmpl($value) '[data-template="recently-viewed-car"]'}}
                {{/each}}
                </div></div>
        {{/if}}
       </script>
       <script data-template="recently-viewed-car" type="text/x-tmpl">
        <div
            class="item"
            title="${brand_name} ${model_name}"
            data-link="${link}"
            data-trackevent-category="Pages"
            data-trackevent-action="Recently-Viewed"
            data-trackevent-label="${brand_name} ${model_name}"
            data-gtm-item
            data-gtm-item-id="${model_id}"
            data-gtm-item-brand="${brand_name }"
            data-gtm-item-model="${model_name}"
            data-gtm-item-name="${brand_name} ${model_name}"
            data-gtm-item-status="${car_state}"
            data-gtm-item-class="${car_class}"
            data-gtm-item-list="Recently Viewed Cars"
            data-gtm-item-position="${itemIndex + 1}"
        ><div><span class="item-img loader-transparent"><img class="owl-lazy"
                         data-src="${image}"
                         src="/i/-.gif"
                         alt="${brand_name} ${model_name}"
                    /></span><a href="${link}" class="h4">${brand_name} ${model_name}</a></div><div>
                {{if car_state == 'ANNONSE' || car_state == 'ANNOUNCE' }}
                    <span class="upcoming-label">Upcoming</span>
                    Expected price
                {{else car_state == 'RUMOURED'}}
                    <span class="upcoming-label">Rumoured</span>
                    Expected price:<br /><span class="bold">Not available</span>
                {{else car_state == 'CONCEPT'}}
                    <span class="upcoming-label">Concept</span>
                    Expected price:<br /><span class="bold">Not available</span>
                {{else}}
                    <div class="rating-star star10" title="Overall rating: ${rating}"><span class="rating-status" style="width: ${rating*20}%;"></span></div><a class="hint" href="${link}reviews/"><b>${reviews_count}</b>&nbsp;reviews</a>
                {{/if}}
            </div>
            {{if car_state != 'RUMOURED' && car_state != 'CONCEPT' }}
                {{if price_min || price_max}}
                    <div
                        data-gtm-item-price-min="${price_min}"
                        data-gtm-item-price-max="${price_max}"
                    >
                        {{if price_range}}
                            <span class="WebRupee"></span> ${price_range}
                        {{else price_min && price_max}}
                            {{if price_max != '0' || price_min != '0'}}
                                <span class="WebRupee"></span> {{html Helper.Price.formatPriceRange(price_min, price_max)}}
                            {{else}}
                                <span class="italic">Not available</span>
                            {{/if}}
                        {{/if}}
                    </div>
                {{/if}}
            {{/if}}
        </div>
       </script>
       <script type="text/javascript">
        var AP = AP || {};
AP.cmd = AP.cmd || [];

(function(){
    function RecentlyViewModels($slot, $template)
    {
        this.$slot = $slot;
        this.$template = $template;
    }

    RecentlyViewModels.prototype.render = function(models, callback)
    {
        this.$slot.one('DOMSubtreeModified', {callback: callback}, this.afterRender);

        if (models.length > 2) {
            this.$template
                    .tmpl({models: models})
                    .appendTo(this.$slot);
        }
    };

    RecentlyViewModels.prototype.afterRender = function (event) {

        if (typeof event.data.callback == 'function') {
            event.data.callback();
        }

    };

    AP.cmd.push(function(container) {
        var recentlyViewModelsService = container.get("recently_view_models_service");
        var eventDispatcher = container.get("event_dispatcher");

        var carouselSettings = {
            margin: 10,
            nav: true,
            dots: false,
            lazyLoad: true,
            responsive: {
                0: {
                    items: 1
                },
                479: {
                    items: 2
                },
                768: {
                    items: 3
                },
                980: {
                    items: 3
                },
                1000: {
                    items: 4
                }
            },
            onRefreshed: function() {
                element.removeClass('d_n');
            }
        };

        var $recentlyViewedTab = $('[data-group="recently-viewed"]');
        var $slot = $('[data-slot="recently-viewed"]');
        var recentlyModels = recentlyViewModelsService.getAll();
        if (recentlyModels.length > 2) {
            $recentlyViewedTab.removeClass('d_n');
        }
        else{
            $recentlyViewedTab.addClass('d_n');
        }

        function renderRecentlyBlock() {
            var $template = $('[data-template="recently-viewed-cars"]');
            var recentlyModelsView = new RecentlyViewModels($slot, $template);

            recentlyModelsView.render(recentlyModels, function() {
                element = $('.carousel_recently_cars');
                element.addClass('d_n')
                element.owlCarousel(carouselSettings);

                setTimeout(function () {
                    eventDispatcher.publish("ModelPage.RecentlyViewed:ready");
                }, 0);
            });
        }

        
            $('[data-type="lazyRender"]').Lazy({
                threshold: 50,
                asyncLoader: function (element) {
                    renderRecentlyBlock();
                    element.load();
                },
                afterLoad: function (element) {
                    element.removeClass('d_n');
                }
            });

        
    });

})();
       </script>
      </section>

            updates on cars and everything related, from across the globe. Here, you will get the latest info on updated
            technology and events from the automotive world.
          </p>

            find the best car and negotiating the price hoping to get the best! Our rich catalogue of new and
           <a href="/upcoming-cars/">
            upcoming cars
           </a>
           gives you immense options to choose from as
            per your need, along with technical specification and price list that you can rely on. Also, if you want to
           <a href="">

           , just give us a chance to inspect it and it
            will be sold within no time!

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var AP = AP || {};
    AP.cmd = AP.cmd || [];

    AP.cmd.push(function (container) {
        var ga = container.get("ga");

        $(document).on("click", "[data-popup-close]", function(e) {
            var target = e.target;

            if (e.target == e.currentTarget && target.hasAttribute("data-popup-close")) {
                e.preventDefault();
                var popupService = container.get("popup_service");
                var popup = popupService.getActivePopup();

                if (popup && popup.has(this)) {
                    popup.close();
                    ga.sendEvent("Popup", "Close");
                }
            }
        });
    });
  </script>
